<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">BiomationScripter - OTProto</h1><a id="user-content-biomationscripter---otproto" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: BiomationScripter - OTProto" href="#biomationscripter---otproto"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Feature Overview</h2><a id="user-content-feature-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Feature Overview" href="#feature-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">OTProto is a module within the BiomationScripter package which contains tools specifically aimed at assisting with scripting protocols for the Opentrons-2. This module makes use of the <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/index.html" rel="nofollow">OT2 API V2</a> python protocol.</p>
<p dir="auto">OTProto contains two submodules:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="#using-otproto"><strong>OTProto:</strong></a> A set of functions and classes which abstract out some parts of the protocol writing, such as determining how many tips are required, and switching loading custom labware</li>
<li><a href="#templates"><strong>OTProto.Templates:</strong></a> A set of classes which generate OT-2 instructions for common protocols, such as plasmid purification and transformation, based on user inputs</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">If you are planning on using the Opentrons to automate common protocols, such as transformation, there may be a pre-written OTProto template available. A list of currently available templates can be found <a href="/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/docs/OTProto_Templates.md">here</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">If you are planning on automating a protocol which you will use many times, but with slightly different variations/inputs, it may be helpful to create your own OTProto template. A walkthrough explaining how this can be done can be found <a href="/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/docs/example_code/OTProto/OTProto-OTProto_Template-Superclass.ipynb">here</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">If you are planning to automate a protocol for which there are no existing templates, and that protocol will only be repeated identically (or not at all), it may be best to not write a template. In this case, the <a href="/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/docs/BiomationScripter.md">general BiomationScripter tools</a> and <a href="#using-otproto">OTProto tools</a> can be used to help write the protocol.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a name="user-content-opentrons-api-names"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">!!! note</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="**Opentrons Labware API Names:**

Throughout this documentation, there will be references to 'Opentrons labware API names'. A full explanation of how labware works in the native Opentrons library can be found [here](https://support.opentrons.com/s/article/Using-labware-in-your-protocols).

Simply, the Opentrons labware API name is used to reference a specific type of labware. For default labware, the API names can be found [here](https://labware.opentrons.com/). For custom labware, it is the name of the definition file (ignoring the .json extension)."><pre class="notranslate"><code>**Opentrons Labware API Names:**

Throughout this documentation, there will be references to 'Opentrons labware API names'. A full explanation of how labware works in the native Opentrons library can be found [here](https://support.opentrons.com/s/article/Using-labware-in-your-protocols).

Simply, the Opentrons labware API name is used to reference a specific type of labware. For default labware, the API names can be found [here](https://labware.opentrons.com/). For custom labware, it is the name of the definition file (ignoring the .json extension).
</code></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Setting up the OT-2 to work with BiomationScripter</h2><a id="user-content-setting-up-the-ot-2-to-work-with-biomationscripter" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Setting up the OT-2 to work with BiomationScripter" href="#setting-up-the-ot-2-to-work-with-biomationscripter"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Due to large amounts of the OT-2's onboard computer being read only, the BiomationScripter package can not be installed as usual. Instead, follow the instructions below to get set up.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Create a new directory called <code>Packages</code> in the writable section of the OT-2's onboard computer
* <code>/var/lib/jupyter/notebooks/</code> is an example of a writable directory</li>
<li>Clone the <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripter">BiomationScripter repo</a> into this new directory</li>
<li>The following code will need to be added to start of every protocol you wish to use BiomationScripter in:
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import sys
sys.path.insert(0, &quot;&lt;Directory&gt;&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">sys</span>
<span class="pl-s1">sys</span>.<span class="pl-c1">path</span>.<span class="pl-c1">insert</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-s">"&lt;Directory&gt;"</span>)</pre></div>
Replace <code>&lt;Directory&gt;</code> with the path you cloned BiomationScripter into (e.g. <code>/var/lib/jupyter/notebooks/Packages/BiomationScripterLib</code>)</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">!!! warning</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Version 6.0.0 of the Opentrons app added in a new analysis function. In order to make use of this function, BiomationScripter must also be installed in a specific location on the controlling PC. Instructions for doing this can be found [here](https://support.opentrons.com/s/article/Using-Python-packages-in-Python-API-protocols#modulenotfounderror). If these instructions are not followed, you will see a 'Protocol analysis failure' popup box, with a message similar to 'No module named BiomationScripter'. Note that you can also choose to ignore this error and proceed to running the protocol."><pre class="notranslate"><code>Version 6.0.0 of the Opentrons app added in a new analysis function. In order to make use of this function, BiomationScripter must also be installed in a specific location on the controlling PC. Instructions for doing this can be found [here](https://support.opentrons.com/s/article/Using-Python-packages-in-Python-API-protocols#modulenotfounderror). If these instructions are not followed, you will see a 'Protocol analysis failure' popup box, with a message similar to 'No module named BiomationScripter'. Note that you can also choose to ignore this error and proceed to running the protocol.
</code></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Using OTProto</h2><a id="user-content-using-otproto" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Using OTProto" href="#using-otproto"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Begin by importing the OTProto module:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import BiomationScripter.OTProto as OTProto"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">BiomationScripter</span>.<span class="pl-v">OTProto</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-v">OTProto</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Functions</h2><a id="user-content-functions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Functions" href="#functions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>add_tip_boxes_to_pipettes</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-add_tip_boxes_to_pipettes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: add_tip_boxes_to_pipettes" href="#function-add_tip_boxes_to_pipettes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This functions calculates how many tip boxes of a specific tip type are required, and then loads that many boxes to the Opentrons deck.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.add_tip_boxes_to_pipettes(protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext, Pipette_Type: str, Tip_Type: str, Tips_Needed: int, Starting_Tip: str)</code> returns <code>float</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
<li><code>Pipette_Type</code> | <code>str</code>: The type of pipette which will use the tips being loaded (either <code>"p20"</code>, <code>"p300"</code>, or <code>"p1000"</code>)</li>
<li><code>Tip_Type</code> | <code>str</code>: The labware <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a> for the type of tip to load (e.g. <code>"opentrons_96_tiprack_20ul"</code>)</li>
<li><code>Tips_Needed</code> | <code>int</code>: Number of tips needed for the entire protocol of the specific tip type</li>
<li><code>Starting_Tip</code> | <code>str = "A1"</code>: The starting tip position in the first tip box, will default to the first position ("A1")</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This function will calculate the number of boxes of the specified tip type needed based on the number of tips needed. The boxes will then be loaded to the Opentrons deck, and associated with the specified pipette type.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>calculate_and_load_labware</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-calculate_and_load_labware" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: calculate_and_load_labware" href="#function-calculate_and_load_labware"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This function calculates how many of a certain labware type is required for a protocol, and then loads the labware to the deck</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.calculate_and_load_labware(protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext, labware_api_name: str, wells_required: int, custom_labware_dir: str = None, label: str = None)</code> returns <code>list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware]</code> and <code>list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well]</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
<li><code>labware_api_name</code> | <code>str</code>: The Opentrons <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a> for the labware to be loaded</li>
<li><code>wells_required</code> | <code>int</code>: The number of wells which need to be available for use</li>
<li><code>custom_labware_dir</code> | <code>str = None</code>: Location of a directory where any custom labware definition files are stored</li>
<li><code>label</code> | <code>str = None</code>: A human readable label for the loaded labware</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This function loads a set of labware, where the type is defined by <code>labware_api_name</code>, and the amount of labware loaded is defined by the number of wells required (as supplied by the <code>wells_required</code> argument).</p>
<p dir="auto">This function first calls <a href="#function-load_labware"><code>BiomationScripter.OTProto.load_labware</code></a> to load a single copy of the labware, as it is assumed that at least one of the labware will always be required. The labware is loaded into the next empty slot on the deck. If not slots remain, an error is raised. This first loaded labware is then used to determine how many wells the labware contains, and therefore how many copies of the labware is required based on the number of wells needed (<code>wells_required</code>). If more than one labware is required, these extra copies are then also loaded onto the next empty slot(s). If at any point there are no more free slots, an error is raised.</p>
<p dir="auto">Once all required labware has been loaded, a list of well locations (<a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware</code></a> is generated. This list of wells locations is equal in length to the number of <code>wells_required</code>, and can be used to determine which wells can be used in each of the loaded labware.</p>
<p dir="auto">The function then returns two variables: the list of loaded labware, and the list of well locations.</p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>custom_labware_dir</code> and <code>labware_api_name</code> arguments are passed directly to <a href="#function-load_labware"><code>BiomationScripter.OTProto.load_labware</code></a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>calculate_tips_needed</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-calculate_tips_needed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: calculate_tips_needed" href="#function-calculate_tips_needed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This function determines how many tips of each size (20uL, 300uL, and 1000uL) are required for a set of liquid transfer actions, based on the pipette types present and whether a new tip should be used for each transfer or not</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.calculate_tips_needed(Protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext, transfers: list[float], template: BMS.OTProto.Template = None, new_tip: bool = True)</code> returns <code>float</code> and <code>float</code> and <code>float</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
<li><code>transfers</code> | <code>list[float]</code>: List of volumes to be transferred by the Opentrons</li>
<li><code>template</code> | <code>BMS.OTProto.template = None</code>: This argument must refer to an OTProto template object - the tips needed will be added to the template's <code>tips_needed</code> attribute as well as returned</li>
<li><code>new_tip</code> | <code>bool = True</code>: A boolean which determines whether a new tip is used for every transfer specified (<code>True</code>), or if one tip is used for all transfers (<code>False</code>)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">For each volume in the list passed to <code>transfers</code>, the <a href="#function-select_pipette_by_volume"><code>select_pipette_by_volume</code></a> function is used to determine which pipette size should be used to perform that transfer, based on the pipette type(s) loaded. It is then determined whether that transfer can be completed in one step (e.g. a p300 transferring 100 uL), or two steps (e.g. a p300 transfering 400 uL in 2*200 uL steps). From this information, along with the <code>new_tip</code> argument, it is determined how many tips are needed for that transfer, and what tip size is required.</p>
<p dir="auto">Once all transfer volumes have been iterated through, the function returns the number of each tip type needed as an <code>int</code> in the order of 20uL, 300uL, and 1000uL.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>dispense_from_aliquots</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-dispense_from_aliquots" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: dispense_from_aliquots" href="#function-dispense_from_aliquots"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This function can be used to dispense varying amounts of liquid from a set of aliquots to a list of destination locations</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.dispense_from_aliquots( protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext, Transfer_Volumes: list[float], Aliquot_Source_Locations: list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well], Destinations: list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well], Min_Tranfer: float = None, Calculate_Only: bool = False, Dead_Volume_Proportion: float = 0.95, Aliquot_Volumes: list[float]/float = None, new_tip: bool = True, mix_after: tuple(int, float/int/str) = None, mix_before: tuple(int, float/int/str) = None, mix_speed_multiplier: float = 1, aspirate_speed_multiplier: float = 1, dispense_speed_multiplier: float = 1, blowout_speed_multiplier: float = 1, touch_tip_source: bool = False, touch_tip_destination: bool = False, blow_out: bool = False, blowout_location: str = "destination well", move_after_dispense: str = None )</code> returns <code>None</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
<li><code>Transfer_Volumes</code> | <code>list[float]</code>: A list of transfer volumes (in microlitres)</li>
<li><code>Aliquot_Source_Locations</code> | <code>list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well]</code>: A list of locations for each of the aliquots - to be used as the potential source locations</li>
<li><code>Destinations</code> | <code>list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well]</code>: A list of locations which liquid will be transferred to</li>
<li><code>Min_Transfer</code> | <code>float = None</code>: The minimal transfer volume to allow - this prevents transfer splits across aliquots from falling below this threshold</li>
<li><code>Calculate_Only</code> | <code>bool = False</code>: The function will only calculate the transfers and return them, rather than perform the liquid handling</li>
<li><code>Dead_Volume_Proportion</code> | <code>float = 0.95</code>: Defines the dead volume proportion of the aliquots - e.g. 0.95 means than 5% of the total well capacity is the dead volume</li>
<li><code>Aliquot_Volumes</code> | <code>list[float]/float = None</code>: A list of volumes relating to the amount of liquid in each aliquot specified by <code>Aliquot_Source_Locations</code> - if a single float is specified this volume will be used for all aliquots</li>
<li><code>new_tip</code> | <code>bool = True</code>: A boolean which determines whether a new tip is used for every transfer specified (<code>True</code>), or if one tip is used for all transfers (<code>False</code>)</li>
<li><code>mix_after</code> | <code>tuple(int, int/float/str) = None</code>: Specifies mixing event after dispensing into the destination location - if <code>None</code>, no mixing occurs - first element in the tuple specifies the number of mixing iterations (aspirate up and down) to occur, and the second element specifies the volume to use in the mixing event (either a volume in microlitres, or the keyword <code>"transfer_volume"</code>, which uses the transfer volume as the mixing volume)</li>
<li><code>mix_before</code> | <code>tuple(int, int/float/str) = None</code>: Specifies mixing event before aspirating from the source location - if <code>None</code>, no mixing occurs - first element in the tuple specifies the number of mixing iterations (aspirate up and down) to occur, and the second element specifies the volume to use in the mixing event (either a volume in microlitres, or the keyword <code>"transfer_volume"</code>, which uses the transfer volume as the mixing volume)</li>
<li><code>mix_speed_multiplier</code> | <code>float = 1</code>: Speed multiplier for mixing steps</li>
<li><code>aspirate_speed_multiplier</code> | <code>float = 1</code>: Speed multiplier for aspirate steps</li>
<li><code>dispense_speed_multiplier</code> | <code>float = 1</code>: Speed multiplier for dispense steps</li>
<li><code>blowout_speed_multiplier</code> | <code>float = 1</code>: Speed multiplier for blowout steps</li>
<li><code>touch_tip_source</code> | <code>bool = False</code>: When true the pipette tip will touch the top, inner sides of the source labware after aspiration</li>
<li><code>touch_tip_destination</code> | <code>bool = False</code>: When true the pipette tip will touch the top, inner sides of the destination labware after dispensing</li>
<li><code>blow_out</code> | <code>bool = False</code>: Defines whether a blowout step will occur</li>
<li><code>blowout_location</code> | <code>str = "destination_well"</code>: Defines where the blowout should occur - ignored if <code>blow_out</code> is <code>False</code></li>
<li><code>move_after_dispense</code> | <code>str = None</code>: Defines if the pipette should move to the <code>"well_top"</code> or <code>"well_bottom"</code> after dispensing, but before any blowout occurs - if <code>None</code> then no movement occurs</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This function determines which aliquots should be used as the source location for the liquid transfer events specified by <code>transfer_liquids</code> and <code>destinations</code>. This information is then passed on to <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/wiki/OTProto#function-transfer_liquids"><code>BiomationScripter.transfer_liquids</code></a> to perform the liquid handling actions.</p>
<p dir="auto">If <code>Aliquot_Volumes</code> isn't <code>None</code>, then volume checking will occur and an error will be raised if there is not enough volume across all aliquots to perform all liquid handling actions. If <code>Aliquot_Volumes</code> is a single float, this volume will be used for all aliquots. If <code>Aliquot_Volumes</code> is a list of floats with a length equal to the number of aliquots, each volumes specified will be used as the amount of liquid in the corresponding aliquot specified by <code>Aliquot_Locations</code></p>
<p dir="auto">If <code>Aliquot_Volumes</code> is left as <code>None</code>, then each aliquot will take turns at being the source location, and no volume checking will occur.</p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>new_tip</code>, <code>mix_after</code>, and <code>mix_before</code> arguments are passed directly to the <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/wiki/OTProto#function-transfer_liquids"><code>BiomationScripter.transfer_liquids</code></a> function.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>get_labware_format</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-get_labware_format" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: get_labware_format" href="#function-get_labware_format"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This function can be used to get the labware format (i.e. number of rows and columns) from an opentrons labware <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.get_labware_format(labware_api_name: str, custom_labware_dir = None)</code> returns <code>(n_rows: int, n_cols: int)</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>labware_api_name</code> | <code>str</code>: Opentrons <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a> for the labware</li>
<li><code>custom_labware_dir</code> | <code>str</code>: Location of any custom labware - only required if simulating away from the OT2</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The function searches through the specified labware's definition file to determine the number of rows and columns, and then returns them. The return order is number or rows first, and then number of columns.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>get_labware_well_capacity</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-get_labware_well_capacity" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: get_labware_well_capacity" href="#function-get_labware_well_capacity"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This function can be used to get a labware's maximum well capacity from an opentrons labware <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.get_labware_well_capacity(labware_api_name: str, custom_labware_dir = None)</code> returns <code>float</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>labware_api_name</code> | <code>str</code>: Opentrons <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a> for the labware</li>
<li><code>custom_labware_dir</code> | <code>str</code>: Location of any custom labware - only required if simulating away from the OT2</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The function searches through the specified labware's definition file to determine the maximum well capacity of the labware, and then returns it. Note that this function may yield unexpected results if the labware has wells with different capacities.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>get_locations</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-get_locations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: get_locations" href="#function-get_locations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Converts well positions in a specified labware to <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well</code></a> objects, which can be used to specify a source or destination location in Opentrons or OTProto liquid handling functions.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.get_locations(Labware: opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware, Wells: list[str]/str, Direction: str = None)</code> returns <code>list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well]</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Labware</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware</code></a>: Labware to generate locations for</li>
<li><code>Wells</code> | <code>list[str]/str</code>: The wells in the specified labware to convert to locations - this can either be a list of wells (<code>["A1", "D5", "E7"]</code>), or a well range (<code>"C2:E4"</code>)</li>
<li><code>Direction</code> | <code>str = None</code>: Used to specify the direction ("Horizontal" or "Vertical") to generate locations when a well range is specified - required when <code>Wells</code> is a well range, ignored when <code>Wells</code> is a list of wells - see <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/wiki/BiomationScripter#function-well_range"><code>BiomationScripter.well_range</code></a> for more information about how directionality works with well ranges</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This function converts a list of wells (or a range of wells) in a specified labware to a list of <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well</code></a> objects (also called locations here). These locations can be used as the source or destination arguments in liquid handling functions such as the opentrons <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext.transfer" rel="nofollow"><code>transfer</code></a> function, or the OTProto <a href="/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/docs"><code>transfer_liquids</code></a> and <a href="/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/docs"><code>dispense_from_aliquots</code></a> functions.</p>
<p dir="auto">If the specified wells are not present in the labware defined by the <code>Labware</code> argument, an error will raised. Also, if <code>Direction</code> is not specified when <code>Wells</code> is a well range, an error will be raised.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>get_p1000</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-get_p1000" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: get_p1000" href="#function-get_p1000"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">!!! note</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="**It is recommended that [`get_pipette`](#function-get_pipette) is used instead**"><pre class="notranslate"><code>**It is recommended that [`get_pipette`](#function-get_pipette) is used instead**
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Returns the p1000 pipette from the supplied <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object if that pipette has been loaded</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.get_p1000(protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext)</code> returns <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Searches the <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object supplied to the <code>protocol</code> argument for a p1000 pipette. If a p1000 single channel pipette has been loaded, it is returned as an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a> object. If the pipette has not been loaded, <code>None</code> is returned.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>get_p20</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-get_p20" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: get_p20" href="#function-get_p20"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">!!! note</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="**It is recommended that [`get_pipette`](#function-get_pipette) is used instead**"><pre class="notranslate"><code>**It is recommended that [`get_pipette`](#function-get_pipette) is used instead**

<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
