</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Searches the <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object supplied to the <code>protocol</code> argument for a p20 pipette. If a p20 single channel pipette has been loaded, it is returned as an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a> object. If the pipette has not been loaded, <code>None</code> is returned.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>get_p300</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-get_p300" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: get_p300" href="#function-get_p300"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">!!! note</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="**It is recommended that [`get_pipette`](#function-get_pipette) is used instead**"><pre class="notranslate"><code>**It is recommended that [`get_pipette`](#function-get_pipette) is used instead**
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Returns the p300 pipette from the supplied <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object if that pipette has been loaded</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.get_p300(protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext)</code> returns <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Searches the <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object supplied to the <code>protocol</code> argument for a p300 pipette. If a p300 single channel pipette has been loaded, it is returned as an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a> object. If the pipette has not been loaded, <code>None</code> is returned.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>get_pipette</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-get_pipette" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: get_pipette" href="#function-get_pipette"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Returns the specified Opentrons pipette as an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a> object if that pipette has been loaded.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.get_pipette(Protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext, Pipette: str)</code> returns <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
<li><code>Pipette</code> | <code>str</code>: The pipette type to return - must be either <code>"p20"</code>, <code>"p300"</code>, or <code>"p1000"</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This function calls the <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/wiki/OTProto#function-get_p20"><code>get_p20</code></a>, <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/wiki/OTProto#function-get_p300"><code>get_p300</code></a>, or <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/wiki/OTProto#function-get_p1000"><code>get_p1000</code></a> function depending on the argument supplied to <code>Pipette</code>, and returns the output.</p>
<p dir="auto">The pipette will only be returned if that pipette type has been loaded to the <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object supplied to the <code>Protocol</code> argument. If the pipette type is not present, <code>None</code> will be returned and no error will be raised.</p>
<p dir="auto">If <code>Pipette</code> is not <code>"p20"</code>, <code>"p300"</code>, or <code>"p1000"</code>, then an error will be raised.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>load_labware_from_layout</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-load_labware_from_layout" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: load_labware_from_layout" href="#function-load_labware_from_layout"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Generates an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware</code></a> object from a <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripter/wiki/BiomationScripter#class-Labware_Layout"><code>BiomationScripter.Labware_Layout</code></a> object</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.load_labware_from_layout(Protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext, Labware_Layout: BiomationScripter.Labware_Layout, deck_position: int = None, custom_labware_dir: str = None)</code> returns <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware</code></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
<li><code>Labware_Layout</code> | <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripter/wiki/BiomationScripter#class-Labware_Layout"><code>BiomationScripter.Labware_Layout</code></a>: The Layout object to be used as the template for generating the <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware</code></a> object</li>
<li><code>deck_position</code> | <code>int = None</code>: An integer (from 1-11) stating which deck position the labware should be loaded on to - if no value is specified, the labware will be loaded onto the next available deck slot</li>
<li><code>custom_labware_dir</code> | <code>str = None</code>: Location of a directory where any custom labware definition files are stored - if not specified then <code>../custom_labware</code> will be used if custom labware is being used</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This function generates and loads an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware</code></a>, which can be used in Opentrons protocols, using a <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripter/wiki/BiomationScripter#class-Labware_Layout"><code>BiomationScripter.Labware_Layout</code></a> as the template. Any content stored in the <code>Labware_Layout.content</code> attribute will not be carried over to the <code>Labware</code> object.</p>
<p dir="auto">For this function to work correctly, the <code>Labware_Layout</code> <code>type</code> attribute (<code>Labware_Layout.type</code>) MUST be the <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a> of the labware to be loaded. If the <code>type</code> attribute can not be found as a labware <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a>, an error will occur.</p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>Labware_Layout.name</code> attribute is used as the label for the <code>Labware</code> object.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>load_labware</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-load_labware" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: load_labware" href="#function-load_labware"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Loads labware (either custom or default) based on an <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.load_labware(parent: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext/opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.TemperatureModuleContext/opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ThermocyclerContext/https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.MagneticModuleContext, labware_api_name: str, deck_position: int = None, custom_labware_dir label: str = None)</code> returns <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware</code></a></p>
<p dir="auto">See the <a href="/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/docs/example_code/OTProto/OTProto-load_labware-Function.ipynb">code snippet examples</a> for example usage.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>load_labware</code> function firstly determines whether the labware type specified by <code>labware_api_name</code> is in the default list of labware, or if it is custom labware. If it is custom, then the <a href="#function-load_custom_labware"><code>load_custom_labware</code></a> function is called and used to load the labware. The <code>custom_labware_dir</code> argument is used to find the custom file location, and if it isn't specified then an error will be raised.</p>
<p dir="auto">The object type supplied to <code>parent</code> determines whether the labware is loaded to the Opentrons deck (when <code>parent</code> is an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object), or to one of the hardware modules (when <code>parent</code> is one of <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.TemperatureModuleContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.TemperatureModuleContext</code></a>/<a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ThermocyclerContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ThermocyclerContext</code></a>/<a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.MagneticModuleContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.MagneticModuleContext</code></a> object).</p>
<p dir="auto">If <code>parent</code> is an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object and <code>deck_position</code> is <code>None</code>, the next empty slot is used (retrieved using <a href="#function-next_empty_slot"><code>OTProto.next_empty_slot</code></a>). If <code>parent</code> is not a <code>ProtocolContext</code> object, then <code>deck_position</code> is ignored.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>load_pipettes_and_tips</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-load_pipettes_and_tips" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: load_pipettes_and_tips" href="#function-load_pipettes_and_tips"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Loads a specified pipette, and creates tip racks which are assigned to that pipette and loads to the deck</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.load_pipettes_and_tips(Protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext, Pipette_Type: str, Pipette_Position: str, Tip_Type: str, Number_Tips_Required: int = None, Starting_Tip: str = "A1")</code> returns <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a> and <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware]</code></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
<li><code>Pipette_Type</code> | <code>str</code>: The <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a> for the pipette type to load (see <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_pipette.html#pipette-models" rel="nofollow">here</a> for pipette types)</li>
<li><code>Pipette_Position</code> | <code>str</code>: The position in which the pipette is loaded (either <code>"left"</code> or <code>"right"</code>)</li>
<li><code>Tip_Type</code> | <code>str</code>: The <a href="#opentrons-api-names">API name</a> for the tip type to load</li>
<li><code>Number_Tips_Required</code> | <code>int = None</code>: The number of <code>Tip_Type</code> tips required in the protocol</li>
<li><code>starting_tip_position</code> | <code>str = "A1"</code>: The first available tip in the first tip rack</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This function will load a pipette of type <code>pipette_type</code> into position <code>Pipette_Position</code> on the Opentrons. Tip racks of type <code>Tip_Type</code> are then loaded to the next empty slot of the Opentrons deck (uses <a href="#function-next_empty_slot"><code>OTProto.next_empty_slot</code></a>) and assigns the tip rack to be used by the pipette just loaded.</p>
<p dir="auto">If <code>Number_Tips_Required = None</code>, then a single tip rack is loaded. If a number is supplied to <code>Number_Tips_Required</code>, the <a href="#function-tip_racks_needed"><code>OTProto.tip_racks_needed</code></a> function is used to determine the number of tip racks to load (<code>Number_Tips_Required</code> and <code>starting_tip_position</code> are passed directly to the <a href="#function-tip_racks_needed"><code>OTProto.tip_racks_needed</code></a> function).</p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>starting_tip_position</code> is used to allow the pipette to know where to begin taking tips from.</p>
<p dir="auto">This function returns two variables: an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a> object which stores information about the pipette and can be used to call liquid handling methods from, and a list of the loaded tip racks as <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware</code></a> objects.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>next_empty_slot</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-next_empty_slot" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: next_empty_slot" href="#function-next_empty_slot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This function gets the next empty slot on the Opentrons deck for the current protocol.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.next_empty_slot(protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext)</code> returns <code>int</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This function gets the <code>deck</code> attribute from the supplied <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object and iterates through each slot on the deck. If there is no labware loaded onto a slot, that slot number is returned as an <code>int</code>. If no empty slots are left, and error is returned.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>select_pipette_by_volume</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-select_pipette_by_volume" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: select_pipette_by_volume" href="#function-select_pipette_by_volume"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Selects the most appropriate loaded pipette for a specified transfer volume.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.select_pipette_by_volume(protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext, Volume: float)</code> returns <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
<li><code>Volume</code> | <code>float</code>: The transfer volume (in microlitres)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This function uses the <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/wiki/OTProto#function-get_p20"><code>get_p20</code></a>, <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/wiki/OTProto#function-get_p300"><code>get_p300</code></a>, or <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/wiki/OTProto#function-get_p1000"><code>get_p1000</code></a> functions to determine which pipettes have been loaded to the <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> supplied to the <code>Protocol</code> argument. From the loaded pipettes, the most appropriate pipette to perform the transfer volume specified by <code>Volume</code> will be returned as an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.InstrumentContext</code></a> object.</p>
<p dir="auto">Note that this function only returns the selected pipette; the transfer action is NOT performed.</p>
<p dir="auto">Pipettes are selected based on whether or not the transfer volume lies within that pipette's volume range. In the case of overlapping volume ranges, the pipette with a lower volume range will be selected to ensure the highest accuracy level (e.g. if both a p20 and p300 are loaded and <code>Volume = 20</code>, the p20 will be returned even though the p300 can transfer 20 uL).</p>
<p dir="auto">If <code>Volume</code> is above the volume range of the largest pipette, the pipette with the largest volume range will be selected (e.g. if a p20 and p300 are loaded and <code>Volume = 400</code>, the p300 will be selected). Note that using a pipette to transfer a volume of liquid higher than its maximum volume range will result in the transfer action being split.</p>
<p dir="auto">If <code>Volume</code> is below 1 uL, an error will be raised as the Opentrons cannot pipette below this volume.</p>
<p dir="auto">If not pipettes are loaded which are suitable for the specified volume, an error will be raised.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>shuffle_locations</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-shuffle_locations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: shuffle_locations" href="#function-shuffle_locations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Takes a list and shuffles the elements within. This generates a message to the robot showing the previous order of the list and the new order of the list. If an output directory is specified, this function will write the lists to a .csv file.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.shuffle_locations(Locations: list[], outdir: str = None, outfile: str = "Locations")</code> returns <code>list[]</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Locations</code> | <code>list[]</code>: A list containing any elements. Typically, this should contain <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well</code></a> objects. May also be invoked upon a list of Wells as strings.</li>
<li><code>outdir</code> | <code>str = None</code>: The path to the output directory where the .csv file will be written. Recommended location is "/data/user_storage/&lt;USER_DIRECTORY&gt;". If this is not specified, the .csv file will not be created.</li>
<li><code>outfile</code> | <code>str = "Locations"</code>: The name that will be used for the .csv file. If this is not specified, the .csv file will be named "Locations" by default.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This function takes a list and shuffles any elements contained within. The new locations will be logged by the robot and shown to the user via the application command line. If an output directory is specified, this information will be written to a .csv file.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>tip_racks_needed</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-tip_racks_needed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: tip_racks_needed" href="#function-tip_racks_needed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Determines the number of tip racks needed based on the number of tips needed, and the first tip available for partially used tip racks</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.tip_racks_needed(tips_needed: int, starting_tip_position: str = "A1")</code> returns <code>int</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>tips_needed</code> | <code>int</code>: Number of tips needed</li>
<li><code>starting_tip_position</code> | <code>str = "A1"</code>: The first available tip in the first tip rack</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>tip_racks_needed</code> returns how many tip racks are needed based on the number of tips needed (<code>tips_needed</code> argument). Only one type of tip should be specified. If two or more tip types are to be used, call this function for each tip type.</p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>starting_tip_position</code> refers to the next available tip position in partially-used racks. All subsequent tip racks following the first rack are assumed to be full. If the tip position doesn't exist in the tip rack, and error is raised.</p>
<p dir="auto">Note that this function doesn't load the tip racks, it just returns the number of tip racks required.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>transfer_liquids</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-transfer_liquids" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: transfer_liquids" href="#function-transfer_liquids"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Transfers liquids from source locations to destination locations</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.transfer_liquids( protocol: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext, Transfer_Volumes: list[float]/float, Source_Locations: list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well]/opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well, Destination_Locations: list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well]/opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well, new_tip: bool = True, mix_after: tuple(int, float/int/str) = None, mix_before: tuple(int, float/int/str) = None, mix_speed_multiplier: float = 1, aspirate_speed_multiplier: float = 1, dispense_speed_multiplier: float = 1, blowout_speed_multiplier: float = 1, touch_tip_source: bool = False, touch_tip_destination: bool = False, blow_out: bool = False, blowout_location: str = "destination well", move_after_dispense: str = None )</code>
returns <code>None</code></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Protocol</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>: The protocol object which is used by the Opentrons API to encapsulate all information relating to the current protocol</li>
<li><code>Transfer_Volumes</code> | <code>list[float]/float</code>: A list of transfer volumes (in microlitres), or a single transfer volume</li>
<li><code>Source_Locations</code> | <code>list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well]</code>/<a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well</code></a>: A list of locations which liquid will be transferred from (can also be a single location)</li>
<li><code>Destination_Locations</code> | <code>list[opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well]</code>/<a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Well</code></a>: A list of locations which liquid will be transferred to (can also be a single location)</li>
<li><code>new_tip</code> | <code>bool = True</code>: A boolean which determines whether a new tip is used for every transfer specified (<code>True</code>), or if one tip is used for all transfers (<code>False</code>)</li>
<li><code>mix_after</code> | <code>tuple(int, int/float/str) = None</code>: Specifies mixing event after dispensing into the destination location - if <code>None</code>, no mixing occurs - first element in the tuple specifies the number of mixing iterations (aspirate up and down) to occur, and the second element specifies the volume to use in the mixing event (either a volume in microlitres, or the keyword <code>"transfer_volume"</code>, which uses the transfer volume as the mixing volume)</li>
<li><code>mix_before</code> | <code>tuple(int, int/float/str) = None</code>: Specifies mixing event before aspirating from the source location - if <code>None</code>, no mixing occurs - first element in the tuple specifies the number of mixing iterations (aspirate up and down) to occur, and the second element specifies the volume to use in the mixing event (either a volume in microlitres, or the keyword <code>"transfer_volume"</code>, which uses the transfer volume as the mixing volume)</li>
<li><code>mix_speed_multiplier</code> | <code>float = 1</code>: Speed multiplier for mixing steps</li>
<li><code>aspirate_speed_multiplier</code> | <code>float = 1</code>: Speed multiplier for aspirate steps</li>
<li><code>dispense_speed_multiplier</code> | <code>float = 1</code>: Speed multiplier for dispense steps</li>
<li><code>blowout_speed_multiplier</code> | <code>float = 1</code>: Speed multiplier for blowout steps</li>
<li><code>touch_tip_source</code> | <code>bool = False</code>: When true the pipette tip will touch the top, inner sides of the source labware after aspiration</li>
<li><code>touch_tip_destination</code> | <code>bool = False</code>: When true the pipette tip will touch the top, inner sides of the destination labware after dispensing</li>
<li><code>blow_out</code> | <code>bool = False</code>: Defines whether a blowout step will occur</li>
<li><code>blowout_location</code> | <code>str = "destination_well"</code>: Defines where the blowout should occur - ignored if <code>blow_out</code> is <code>False</code></li>
<li><code>move_after_dispense</code> | <code>str = None</code>: Defines if the pipette should move to the <code>"well_top"</code> or <code>"well_bottom"</code> after dispensing, but before any blowout occurs - if <code>None</code> then no movement occurs</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>transfer_liquids</code> function is intended to generate liquid transfer actions for the <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object supplied by <code>Protocol</code>. A liquid transfer action is generated for each element in the list of volumes specified by the <code>Transfer_Volumes</code> argument. The source for the transfer is determined by using the element in <code>Source_Locations</code> with the same index as the volume specified in <code>Transfer_Volumes</code>, and the destination is determined in the same way, but using <code>Destination_Locations</code>. So for example, if <code>Transfer_Volumes = [20, 100, 400]</code>, <code>Source_Locations = [Source_1, Source_1, Source_2]</code>, and <code>Destination_Locations = [Dest_1, Dest_2, Dest_3]</code>, then the following three transfer actions will be generated:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Transfer 20 uL from <code>Source_1</code> to <code>Dest_1</code></li>
<li>Transfer 100 uL from <code>Source_1</code> to <code>Dest_2</code></li>
<li>Transfer 400 uL from <code>Source_2</code> to <code>Dest_3</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">The <code>new_tip</code> argument determines whether a new tip is used for each transfer action, or if the same tip is used for all transfers. The <code>new_tip</code>, <code>mix_before</code>, and <code>mix_after</code> arguments apply to all transfer actions. If different transfers require different behaviours, it is recommended to split the transfers and call the <code>transfer_liquids</code> function for each scenario.</p>
<p dir="auto">For each transfer action, <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/wiki/OTProto#function-select_pipette_by_volume"><code>select_pipette_by_volume</code></a> is used to determine the best pipette to use from those which have been loaded. If no suitable pipettes are present, an error will be raised. If the transfer volume is larger than the volume range of the largest pipette loaded, the transfer action is split into two. For example, if a p20 and p300 are loaded, and a transfer volume of 400 uL is specified, two transfer actions of 200uL will occur. If <code>new_tip = True</code>, a new tip will be used for both transfer actions. If <code>new_tip = False</code>, the same tip will be used.</p>
<p dir="auto">If the length of <code>Transfer_Volumes</code>, <code>Source_Locations</code>, and <code>Destination_Locations</code> are not all identical, an error will be rasied.</p>
<p dir="auto">It is possible to supply a single transfer volume, source location, and destination location without making them into a list (e.g. <code>Transfer_Volumes = 20</code>, <code>Source_Locations = source_1</code>, and <code>Destination_Locations = dest_1</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Function: <a href="https://github.com/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/BiomationScripter/OTProto/__init__.py"><code>load_custom_labware</code></a></h3><a id="user-content-function-load_custom_labware" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Function: load_custom_labware" href="#function-load_custom_labware"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">⚠️</g-emoji> <strong>This function shouldn't need to be called directly. It is used by <a href="#function-load_labware"><code>Load_Labware</code></a></strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">This function loads a custom labware from a specified <code>.json</code> labware file created using the <a href="https://labware.opentrons.com/create/" rel="nofollow">Opentrons Labware Creator</a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>OTProto.load_custom_labware(parent: opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext/opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.TemperatureModuleContext/opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ThermocyclerContext/https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.MagneticModuleContext, file: str, deck_position: int = None, label: str = None)</code> returns <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware</code></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Arguments:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>parent</code> | <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a>/<a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.TemperatureModuleContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.TemperatureModuleContext</code></a>/<a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ThermocyclerContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ThermocyclerContext</code></a>/<a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.MagneticModuleContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.MagneticModuleContext</code></a>: Specifies onto what the labware should be loaded - <code>ProtocolContext</code> is used to load onto the Opentrons deck, and a <code>ModuleContext</code> is used to load the labware onto a hardware module (e.g. temperature module), rather than the deck</li>
<li><code>file</code> | <code>str</code>: The location of the <code>.json</code> labware file (should be the full path to the file, including the file name and file extension)</li>
<li><code>deck_position</code> | <code>int = None</code>: The deck position to load the labware to</li>
<li><code>label</code> | <code>str = None</code>: A human-readable name for the labware</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Behaviour:</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Labware defined by the labware file supplied by the <code>file</code> argument is loaded and returned as a <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.labware.Labware</code></a> object. If the labware file cannot be found at the location specified by the <code>file</code> argument, an error will occur.</p>
<p dir="auto">The object type supplied to <code>parent</code> determines whether the labware is loaded to the Opentrons deck (when <code>parent</code> is an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object), or to one of the hardware modules (when <code>parent</code> is one of <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.TemperatureModuleContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.TemperatureModuleContext</code></a>/<a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ThermocyclerContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ThermocyclerContext</code></a>/<a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.MagneticModuleContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.MagneticModuleContext</code></a> object).</p>
<p dir="auto">If <code>parent</code> is an <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/new_protocol_api.html#opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext" rel="nofollow"><code>opentrons.protocol_api.contexts.ProtocolContext</code></a> object and <code>deck_position</code> is <code>None</code>, the next empty slot is used (retrieved using <a href="#function-next_empty_slot"><code>OTProto.next_empty_slot</code></a>). If <code>parent</code> is not a <code>ProtocolContext</code> object, then <code>deck_position</code> is ignored.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">OTProto Templates</h2><a id="user-content-otproto-templates" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: OTProto Templates" href="#otproto-templates"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">BiomationScripter Templates can be used to help quickly and easily generate automation protocols for common experiments or procedures. Protocols generated using the same Template will all follow the same basic instructions, but will differ depending on user inputs. For example, the heat shock transformation Template accepts user inputs for aspects such as the length of the heat shock, the final volume of the transformations, and the DNA to use in each transformation.</p>
<p dir="auto">See the full documentation <a href="/intbio-ncl/BiomationScripterLib/blob/main/docs/OTProto_Templates.md">here</a></p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Simulating Protocols</h2><a id="user-content-simulating-protocols" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Simulating Protocols" href="#simulating-protocols"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Protocols can be simulated on any computer which has the <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/writing.html#installing" rel="nofollow">Opentrons API installed</a>. There are two methods of simulating protocols written using BiomationScripter.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Within the python script:</h3><a id="user-content-within-the-python-script" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Within the python script:" href="#within-the-python-script"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This method of simulating the protocol requires a slight addition to the python script, and may be useful when writing protocols using Jupyter Notebook or in an interactive environment.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Add the following lines to the end of your python script:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from opentrons import simulate as OT2 # Import the simulation module from the API
protocol = OT2.get_protocol_api('2.10') # Create the protocol object with the correct API version
protocol.home() # Simulating homing the pipetting head
run(protocol) # Call your 'run' function to run the protocol
# Print out each action that the opentrons will perform when running your protocol
for line in protocol.commands():
    print(line)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">opentrons</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">simulate</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-v">OT2</span> <span class="pl-c"># Import the simulation module from the API</span>
<span class="pl-s1">protocol</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">OT2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_protocol_api</span>(<span class="pl-s">'2.10'</span>) <span class="pl-c"># Create the protocol object with the correct API version</span>
<span class="pl-s1">protocol</span>.<span class="pl-c1">home</span>() <span class="pl-c"># Simulating homing the pipetting head</span>
<span class="pl-en">run</span>(<span class="pl-s1">protocol</span>) <span class="pl-c"># Call your 'run' function to run the protocol</span>
<span class="pl-c"># Print out each action that the opentrons will perform when running your protocol</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">line</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">protocol</span>.<span class="pl-c1">commands</span>():
    <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">line</span>)</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Save and run this modified script.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>IMPORTANT</strong> Make sure that these changes are reverted before uploading to the Opentrons, otherwise you will get errors.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">From the command line:</h3><a id="user-content-from-the-command-line" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: From the command line:" href="#from-the-command-line"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This method of simulating the protocol does not require the python script to be modified.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Follow the instructions from the <a href="https://docs.opentrons.com/v2/writing.html#simulating-your-scripts" rel="nofollow">Opentrons API documentation</a>.</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note</strong> For protocols which use template classes, give the <code>Simulate</code> variable as <code>False</code>, or simply don't declare it, when simulating using this method.</p>
